(prog (expr (expr source) ( (sublist (sub (expr 'avaliacao.R'))) )) \r\n \r\n # INICIALIZACAO DA POPULACAO E GERACAO DE INDIVIDUOS\r\n # entrada: Saida da funcao entrada\r\n # nSINTETICA: Variavel global com o tamanho da serie sintetica\r\n \r\n # GERACAO DE UM INIDIVIDUO ALEATORIAMENTE\r\n (expr (expr geraIndividuo) = (expr function ( (formlist (form entrada) , (form lags)) ) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr (expr (expr nINDIVIDUO) = (expr sum)) ( (sublist (sub (expr lags))) )) * (expr 12)) \r\n (expr (expr individuoMIN) = (expr - (expr 1))) \r\n (expr (expr individuoMAX) = (expr 1)) \r\n (expr (expr (expr individuo) = (expr runif)) ( (sublist (sub (expr nINDIVIDUO)) , (sub (expr individuoMIN)) , (sub (expr individuoMAX))) )) \r\n (expr (expr (expr momentos) = (expr momentos)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr individuo)) , (sub (expr lags)) , (sub (expr nSINTETICA))) )) \r\n \r\n # ENQUANTO AS AVALICOES ESTOURAREM, E PROCURADO OYUTRO INDIVIDUO\r\n (expr while ( (expr (expr estouro) ( (sublist (sub (expr momentos))) )) ) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr (expr individuo) = (expr runif)) ( (sublist (sub (expr nINDIVIDUO)) , (sub (expr individuoMIN)) , (sub (expr individuoMAX))) )) \r\n (expr (expr (expr momentos) = (expr momentos)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr individuo)) , (sub (expr lags)) , (sub (expr nSINTETICA))) )) \r\n) })) \r\n (expr (expr (expr avaliacao) = (expr avaliacao)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr momentos))) )) \r\n \r\n (expr (expr (expr final) = (expr list)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr individuo) = (expr individuo))) , (sub (expr (expr serie) = (expr (expr momentos) $ (expr serie)))) , (sub (expr (expr avaliacao) = (expr avaliacao)))) )) \r\n (expr (expr return) ( (sublist (sub (expr final))) )) \r\n) }))) \r\n \r\n # AVALIACAO DE UM INDIVIDUO JA OBTIDO\r\n (expr (expr avaliaIndividuo) = (expr function ( (formlist (form entrada) , (form lags) , (form individuo)) ) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr (expr momentos) = (expr momentos)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr individuo)) , (sub (expr lags)) , (sub (expr nSINTETICA))) )) \r\n (expr if ( (expr (expr estouro) ( (sublist (sub (expr momentos))) )) ) (expr (expr return) ( (sublist (sub (expr NULL))) ))) \r\n \r\n (expr (expr (expr avaliacao) = (expr avaliacao)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr momentos))) )) \r\n \r\n (expr (expr (expr final) = (expr list)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr individuo) = (expr individuo))) , (sub (expr (expr serie) = (expr (expr momentos) $ (expr serie)))) , (sub (expr (expr avaliacao) = (expr avaliacao)))) )) \r\n (expr (expr return) ( (sublist (sub (expr final))) )) \r\n) }))) \r\n \r\n # GERACAO DA POPULACAO\r\n #**UTILIZA CLUSTERIZACAO**\r\n (expr (expr geraPopulacao) = (expr function ( (formlist (form entrada) , (form lags) , (form parametrosIniciais) , (form nP)) ) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr (expr populacao) = (expr list)) ( (sublist sub) )) \r\n \r\n # CASO NAO HAJA PARAMETROS INICIAIS, SAO GERADOS ALEATORIAMENTE\r\n (expr if ( (expr (expr is.null) ( (sublist (sub (expr parametrosIniciais))) )) ) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr p) = (expr (expr 1) : (expr nP))) \r\n (expr (expr (expr populacao) = (expr lapply)) ( (sublist (sub (expr p)) , (sub (expr (expr function ( (formlist (form x)) ) (expr geraIndividuo)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr lags))) )))) )) \r\n) })) \r\n \r\n) else))) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr p) = (expr (expr 1) : (expr ( (expr (expr ( (expr (expr length) ( (sublist (sub (expr parametrosIniciais))) )) )) / (expr ( (expr (expr 12) * (expr ( (expr (expr sum) ( (sublist (sub (expr lags))) )) ))) ))) )))) \r\n (expr (expr (expr populacao) = (expr parLapply)) ( (sublist (sub (expr cl)) , (sub (expr p)) , (sub (expr (expr function ( (formlist (form x)) ) (expr avaliaIndividuo)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr lags)) , (sub (expr (expr parametrosIniciais) [ (sublist (sub (expr x)) , sub) ]))) )))) )) \r\n # SAO RETIRADOS OS QUE HOUVERAM ESTOURO\r\n (expr (expr populacao) = (expr (expr populacao) [ (sublist (sub (expr (expr (expr lengths) ( (sublist (sub (expr populacao))) )) != (expr 0)))) ])) \r\n \r\n # CASO NAO SEJAM O BASTANTE, OS DEMAIS SAO GERADOS POR CROSSOVER\r\n (expr if ( (expr (expr ( (expr (expr length) ( (sublist (sub (expr populacao))) )) )) < (expr nP)) ) (expr { (exprlist (expr (expr print) ( (sublist (sub (expr "gerando crossover entre os individuos..."))) )) \r\n (expr (expr n) = (expr (expr nP) - (expr ( (expr (expr length) ( (sublist (sub (expr populacao))) )) )))) \r\n (expr (expr (expr populacao) = (expr completaPopulacao)) ( (sublist (sub (expr entrada)) , (sub (expr lags)) , (sub (expr populacao)) , (sub (expr n))) )) \r\n) })) \r\n) }) \r\n \r\n (expr (expr print) ( (sublist (sub (expr "populacao completa!"))) )) \r\n (expr (expr return) ( (sublist (sub (expr populacao))) )) \r\n } \r\n \r\n completaPopulacao = function ( entrada , lags , populacao , n ) { p = 1 : n \r\n \r\n populacaoRestante = list ( ) \r\n populacaoRestante = lapply ( p , function ( x ) cruzamentoBLX ( entrada , lags , populacao , 1 , - 1 ) ) \r\n \r\n populacaoFinal = c ( populacao , populacaoRestante ) \r\n return ( populacaoFinal ) \r\n } \r\n \r\n # CRUZAMENTO BLX ENTRE OS INDIVIDUOS\r\n #**UTILIZA CLUSTERIZACAO**\r\n geraCruzamento = function ( entrada , lags , populacao , Pc , Pm , nP ) { p = 1 : nP \r\n \r\n # E GERADA UMA NOVA POPULACAO ATRAVES DOS OPERADORES DE CRUZAMENTO\r\n novaPopulacao = list ( ) \r\n novaPopulacao = parLapply ( cl , p , function ( x ) cruzamentoBLX ( entrada , lags , populacao , Pc , Pm ) ) \r\n \r\n return ( novaPopulacao ) \r\n } \r\n \r\n # CRUZAMENTO COM UMA PROBABILIDADE Pc DE CRUZAMENTO E Pm DE MUTACAO\r\n cruzamentoBLX = function ( entrada , lags , populacao , Pc , Pm ) { nINDIVIDUO = sum ( lags ) * 12 \r\n \r\n if ( ( runif ( 1 , 0 , 1 ) ) < Pm ) { individuo = geraIndividuo ( entrada , lags ) \r\n return ( individuo ) \r\n } \r\n \r\n ALFA = 0.5 \r\n beta = runif ( nINDIVIDUO , - ALFA , 1 + ALFA ) \r\n homog = runif ( nINDIVIDUO , 0 , 1 ) <= Pc \r\n \r\n pais = torneio ( 3 , length ( populacao ) ) \r\n pai1 = populacao [[ pais [ 1 ] ] ] $ individuo \r\n pai2 = populacao [[ pais [ 2 ] ] ] $ individuo \r\n \r\n filho = pai1 + homog * beta * ( pai2 - pai1 ) \r\n momentos = momentos ( entrada , filho , lags , nSINTETICA ) \r\n \r\n while ( estouro ( momentos ) ) { pais = torneio ( 3 , length ( populacao ) ) \r\n pai1 = populacao [[ pais [ 1 ] ] ] $ individuo \r\n pai2 = populacao [[ pais [ 2 ] ] ] $ individuo \r\n \r\n filho = pai1 + homog * beta * ( pai2 - pai1 ) \r\n momentos = momentos ( entrada , filho , lags , nSINTETICA ) \r\n } \r\n avaliacao = avaliacao ( entrada , momentos ) \r\n \r\n final = list ( individuo = filho , serie = momentos $ serie , avaliacao = avaliacao ) \r\n return ( final ) \r\n } \r\n \r\n # ESCOLHA DOS INDIVIDUOS POR TORNEIO\r\n torneio = function ( nPossibilidades , n ) { nPossibilidades = min ( nPossibilidades , n ) \r\n possiveis = sample ( n , nPossibilidades , replace = F ) \r\n possiveis = sort ( possiveis ) \r\n possiveis = possiveis [ 1 : 2 ] \r\n \r\n return ( possiveis ) \r\n })

(prog \n \n # Comments start with number symbols.\n \n # You can't make multi-line comments,\n # but you can stack multiple comments like so.\n \n # in Windows you can use CTRL-ENTER to execute a line.\n # on Mac it is COMMAND-ENTER\n \n \n \n #############################################################################\n # Stuff you can do without understanding anything about programming\n #############################################################################\n \n # In this section, we show off some of the cool stuff you can do in\n # R without understanding anything about programming. "numeric"\n (expr (expr class) ( (sublist (sub (expr - (expr Inf)))) )) # "numeric"\n # You might use "Inf", for example, in integrate(dnorm, 3, Inf);\n # this obviates Z-score tables.\n \n # BASIC ARITHMETIC\n # 49.2    # numeric minus numeric gives numeric\n (expr (expr 2.0) * (expr 2L)) # 4       # numeric times integer gives numeric\n (expr (expr 3L) / (expr 4)) # 0.75    # integer over numeric gives numeric\n (expr (expr 3) %% (expr 2)) # 1       # the remainder of two numerics is another numeric\n # Illegal arithmetic yields you a "not-a-number":\n (expr (expr 0) / (expr 0)) # NaN\n (expr (expr class) ( (sublist (sub (expr NaN))) )) # "numeric"\n # You can do arithmetic on two vectors with length greater than 1,\n # so long as the larger vector's length is an integer multiple of the smaller\n (expr (expr (expr (expr c) ( (sublist (sub (expr 1)) , (sub (expr 2)) , (sub (expr 3))) )) + (expr c)) ( (sublist (sub (expr 1)) , (sub (expr 2)) , (sub (expr 3))) )) # 2 4 6\n # Since a single number is a vector of length one, scalars are applied \n # elementwise to vectors\n (expr (expr ( (expr (expr (expr (expr 4) * (expr c)) ( (sublist (sub (expr 1)) , (sub (expr 2)) , (sub (expr 3))) )) - (expr 2)) )) / (expr 2)) # (expr plyr)) \n \n \n \n #########################\n # Loading data\n #########################\n \n # "pets.csv" is a file on the internet\n # (but it could just as easily be a file on your own computer)\n (expr (expr require) ( (sublist (sub (expr RCurl))) )) \n (expr (expr (expr pets) <- (expr read.csv)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr textConnection) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr getURL) ( (sublist (sub (expr "https://learnxinyminutes.com/docs/pets.csv"))) )))) )))) )) \n (expr pets) \n (expr (expr head) ( (sublist (sub (expr pets)) , (sub (expr 2))) )) # first two rows\n (expr (expr tail) ( (sublist (sub (expr pets)) , (sub (expr 1))) )) # last row\n \n # To save a data frame or matrix as a .csv file\n (expr (expr write.csv) ( (sublist (sub (expr pets)) , (sub (expr "pets2.csv"))) )) # to make a new .csv file\n # set working directory with setwd(), look it up with getwd()\n \n # Try ?read.csv and ?write.csv for more information\n \n \n \n #########################\n # Statistical Analysis\n #########################\n \n # Linear regression!\n (expr (expr (expr linearModel) <- (expr lm)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr price) ~ (expr time))) , (sub (expr (expr data) = (expr list1)))) )) \n (expr linearModel) # outputs result of regression\n # =>\n # Call:\n # lm(formula = price ~ time, data = list1)\n # \n # Coefficients:\n # (Intercept)         time  \n #      0.1453       0.4943  \n (expr (expr summary) ( (sublist (sub (expr linearModel))) )) # more verbose output from the regression\n # =>\n # Call:\n # lm(formula = price ~ time, data = list1)\n #\n # Residuals:\n #     Min      1Q  Median      3Q     Max \n # -8.3134 -3.0131 -0.3606  2.8016 10.3992 \n #\n # Coefficients:\n #             Estimate Std. Error t value Pr(>|t|)    \n # (Intercept)  0.14527    1.50084   0.097    0.923    \n # time         0.49435    0.06379   7.749 2.44e-09 ***\n # ---\n # Signif. codes:  0 ‘***’ 0.001 ‘**’ 0.01 ‘*’ 0.05 ‘.’ 0.1 ‘ ’ 1\n #\n # Residual standard error: 4.657 on 38 degrees of freedom\n # Multiple R-squared:  0.6124,\tAdjusted R-squared:  0.6022 \n # F-statistic: 60.05 on 1 and 38 DF,  p-value: 2.44e-09\n (expr (expr coef) ( (sublist (sub (expr linearModel))) )) # extract estimated parameters\n # =>\n # (Intercept)        time \n #   0.1452662   0.4943490 \n (expr (expr (expr summary) ( (sublist (sub (expr linearModel))) )) $ (expr coefficients)) # another way to extract results\n # =>\n #              Estimate Std. Error    t value     Pr(>|t|)\n # (Intercept) 0.1452662 1.50084246 0.09678975 9.234021e-01\n # time        0.4943490 0.06379348 7.74920901 2.440008e-09\n (expr (expr (expr summary) ( (sublist (sub (expr linearModel))) )) $ (expr (expr coefficients) [ (sublist sub , (sub (expr 4))) ])) # the p-values \n # =>\n #  (Intercept)         time \n # 9.234021e-01 2.440008e-09 \n \n # GENERAL LINEAR MODELS\n # Logistic regression\n (expr (expr set.seed) ( (sublist (sub (expr 1))) )) \n (expr (expr (expr (expr list1) $ (expr success)) = (expr rbinom)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr length) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr list1) $ (expr time)))) ))) , (sub (expr 1)) , (sub (expr .5))) )) # random binary\n (expr (expr (expr glModel) <- (expr glm)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr success) ~ (expr time))) , (sub (expr (expr data) = (expr list1))) , (sub (expr (expr (expr family) = (expr binomial)) ( (sublist (sub (expr (expr link) = (expr "logit")))) )))) )) \n (expr glModel) # outputs result of logistic regression\n # =>\n # Call:  glm(formula = success ~ time, \n #\tfamily = binomial(link = "logit"), data = list1)\n #\n # Coefficients:\n # (Intercept)         time  \n #     0.17018     -0.01321  \n # \n # Degrees of Freedom: 39 Total (i.e. Null);  38 Residual\n # Null Deviance:\t    55.35 \n # Residual Deviance: 55.12 \t AIC: 59.12\n (expr (expr summary) ( (sublist (sub (expr glModel))) )) # more verbose output from the regression\n # =>\n # Call:\n # glm(formula = success ~ time, \n #\tfamily = binomial(link = "logit"), data = list1)\n \n # Deviance Residuals: \n #    Min      1Q  Median      3Q     Max  \n # -1.245  -1.118  -1.035   1.202   1.327  \n # \n # Coefficients:\n #             Estimate Std.
